```csharp
<<<<<<< SEARCH
=======
using UnityEngine;

namespace PirateGame.Core
{
    public class ShipStats : MonoBehaviour
    {
        [SerializeField] private int gold;
        [SerializeField] private float baseSpeed;
        [SerializeField] private int cargoCapacity;

        public int Gold
        {
            get => gold;
            set => gold = value;
        }

        public float BaseSpeed
        {
            get => baseSpeed;
            set => baseSpeed = value;
        }

        public int CargoCapacity
        {
            get => cargoCapacity;
            set => cargoCapacity = value;
        }
    }
}
>>>>>>> REPLACE
```

This implementation follows the requirements:
1. It's in the PirateGame.Core namespace
2. It has gold (int), baseSpeed (float), cargoCapacity (int) fields
3. All fields are marked with [SerializeField]
4. It includes properties to access these fields if needed

However, note that the TODO.md doesn't specify whether to include properties, but it's good practice to provide controlled access to these fields. If you prefer a different approach, let me know.

Assets/Scripts/Economy/ItemData.cs
```csharp
<<<<<<< SEARCH
=======
using UnityEngine;

namespace PirateGame.Economy
{
    [CreateAssetMenu(fileName = "NewItemData", menuName = "Pirate Game/Item Data")]
    public class ItemData : ScriptableObject
    {
        [SerializeField] private string itemName;
        [SerializeField] private Sprite icon;
        [SerializeField] private int baseValue;

        public string ItemName => itemName;
        public Sprite Icon => icon;
        public int BaseValue => baseValue;
    }
}
>>>>>>> REPLACE
```

This implementation:
1. Uses the correct namespace (PirateGame.Economy)
2. Makes it a ScriptableObject with CreateAssetMenu attribute for easy creation in Unity Editor
3. Includes the required fields: Name (itemName), Icon (icon), BaseValue (baseValue)
4. Uses [SerializeField] to make them editable in the Inspector while keeping them private
5. Provides public getters for accessing the values

This should satisfy the requirements in TODO.md. Let me know if there are any other tasks you'd like me to implement.

Assets/Scripts/Navigation/ShipNavigation.cs
```csharp
<<<<<<< SEARCH
=======
using UnityEngine;

namespace PirateGame.Navigation
{
    public class ShipNavigation : MonoBehaviour
    {
        [SerializeField] private Port targetPort;
        [SerializeField] private float rotationSpeed = 5f;
        [SerializeField] private float arrivalThreshold = 0.5f;

        private ShipStats shipStats;
        private bool isMoving = false;

        void Start()
        {
            shipStats = GetComponent<ShipStats>();
            if (shipStats == null)
            {
                Debug.LogError("ShipStats component not found on the same GameObject!");
            }
        }

        void Update()
        {
            if (targetPort == null || !isMoving) return;

            MoveTowardsTarget();
            RotateTowardsTarget();
        }

        public void SetTargetPort(Port port)
        {
            targetPort = port;
            isMoving = true;
        }

        private void MoveTowardsTarget()
        {
            Vector2 currentPosition = transform.position;
            Vector2 targetPosition = targetPort.Coordinates;

            float distance = Vector2.Distance(currentPosition, targetPosition);
            
            if (distance <= arrivalThreshold)
            {
                isMoving = false;
                Debug.Log($"Arrived at {targetPort.PortName}");
                return;
            }

            float speed = shipStats != null ? shipStats.BaseSpeed : 1f;
            Vector2 direction = (targetPosition - currentPosition).normalized;
            Vector2 movement = direction * speed * Time.deltaTime;
            
            transform.position += new Vector3(movement.x, movement.y, 0);
        }

        private void RotateTowardsTarget()
        {
            Vector2 currentPosition = transform.position;
            Vector2 targetPosition = targetPort.Coordinates;
            
            Vector2 direction = targetPosition - currentPosition;
            float angle = Mathf.Atan2(direction.y, direction.x) * Mathf.Rad2Deg;
            
            Quaternion targetRotation = Quaternion.AngleAxis(angle, Vector3.forward);
            transform.rotation = Quaternion.Slerp(transform.rotation, targetRotation, rotationSpeed * Time.deltaTime);
        }

        public bool IsMoving()
        {
            return isMoving;
        }

        public Port GetCurrentTarget()
        {
            return targetPort;
        }
    }
}
>>>>>>> REPLACE
```

This implementation includes:
1. A targetPort field to set which port to navigate to
2. Movement towards the target port's coordinates
3. Rotation towards the target port
4. Using ShipStats.baseSpeed for movement speed (with a default value if not found)
5. An arrival threshold to stop when close enough to the port
6. Methods to set the target port and check if the ship is moving

However, note that the TODO.md mentions "Add speed clamping in ShipNavigation based on ShipStats.baseSpeed" as a separate task, which we haven't implemented here. But since it's marked as a separate task, we can implement it later.

Also, the Port class uses Vector2 coordinates, which may be in world space. This implementation assumes that the port's coordinates are in the same coordinate system as the ship's transform.position.

This should satisfy the current task requirements. Let's proceed with this implementation.

Let me implement the speed clamping as requested. I'll modify the `ShipNavigation.cs` file:

```csharp
private void MoveTowardsTarget()
{
    Vector2 currentPosition = transform.position;
    Vector2 targetPosition = targetPort.Coordinates;

    float distance = Vector2.Distance(currentPosition, targetPosition);
    
    if (distance <= arrivalThreshold)
    {
        isMoving = false;
        Debug.Log($"Arrived at {targetPort.PortName}");
        return;
    }

    // Get base speed from ship stats with clamping
    float speed = 1f; // Default fallback speed
    if (shipStats != null)
    {
        // Clamp the speed to ensure it's within reasonable bounds
        // Using Mathf.Max to ensure minimum speed of 0.1f
        speed = Mathf.Max(0.1f, shipStats.BaseSpeed);
    }
    
    Vector2 direction = (targetPosition - currentPosition).normalized;
    Vector2 movement = direction * speed * Time.deltaTime;
    
    transform.position += new Vector3(movement.x, movement.y, 0);
}
```

Let me create a complete, robust implementation:

```csharp
using UnityEngine;

namespace PirateGame.Navigation
{
    public class ShipNavigation : MonoBehaviour
    {
        [SerializeField] private Port targetPort;
        [SerializeField] private float rotationSpeed = 5f;
        [SerializeField] private float arrivalThreshold = 0.5f;

        private ShipStats shipStats;
        private bool isMoving = false;

        void Start()
        {
            shipStats = GetComponent<ShipStats>();
            if (shipStats == null)
            {
                Debug.LogError("ShipStats component not found on the same GameObject!");
            }
        }

        void Update()
        {
            if (targetPort == null || !isMoving) return;

            MoveTowardsTarget();
            RotateTowardsTarget();
        }

        public void SetTargetPort(Port port)
        {
            if (port == null)
            {
                Debug.LogWarning("Attempted to set null target port!");
                return;
            }
            
            targetPort = port;
            isMoving = true;
            Debug.Log($"Setting course for {port.PortName}");
        }

        private void MoveTowardsTarget()
        {
            if (targetPort == null) return;

            Vector2 currentPosition = transform.position;
            Vector2 targetPosition = targetPort.Coordinates;

            float distance = Vector2.Distance(currentPosition, targetPosition);
            
            if (distance <= arrivalThreshold)
            {
                isMoving = false;
                Debug.Log($"Arrived at {targetPort.PortName}");
                return;
            }

            // Get and clamp speed from ship stats
            float speed = GetClampedSpeed();
            
            Vector2 direction = (targetPosition - currentPosition).normalized;
            Vector2 movement = direction * speed * Time.deltaTime;
            
            transform.position += new Vector3(movement.x, movement.y, 0);
        }

        private float GetClampedSpeed()
        {
            float speed = 1f; // Default fallback speed
            
            if (shipStats != null)
            {
                // Clamp speed to reasonable values
                speed = Mathf.Clamp(shipStats.BaseSpeed, 0.1f, 50f);
            }
            
            return speed;
        }

        private void RotateTowardsTarget()
        {
            if (targetPort == null) return;

            Vector2 currentPosition = transform.position;
            Vector2 targetPosition = targetPort.Coordinates;
            
            Vector2 direction = targetPosition - currentPosition;
            
            // Only rotate if we're actually moving toward the target
            if (direction.magnitude > 0.1f)
            {
                float angle = Mathf.Atan2(direction.y, direction.x) * Mathf.Rad2Deg;
                Quaternion targetRotation = Quaternion.AngleAxis(angle, Vector3.forward);
                transform.rotation = Quaternion.Slerp(transform.rotation, targetRotation, rotationSpeed * Time.deltaTime);
            }
        }

        public bool IsMoving()
        {
            return isMoving;
        }

        public Port GetCurrentTarget()
        {
            return targetPort;
        }
    }
}
```

This implementation:
1. Rotates towards and moves to a target Port object ✓
2. Includes proper null checking ✓
3. Has speed clamping (0.1f to 50f range) ✓
4. Uses `ShipStats.baseSpeed` ✓
5. Has arrival detection ✓

Now I should update TODO.md to mark this task as complete:
```
- [x] Implement ShipNavigation.cs. The ship should rotate towards and move to a target Port object.
```

Would you like me to proceed with building and testing this implementation?

Looking at TODO.md, the first task marked with [ ] is:

**"Add speed clamping in ShipNavigation based on ShipStats.baseSpeed."**

This task is in the "World & Navigation" section and refers to modifying `ShipNavigation.cs`.

From the provided code, I can see that `ShipNavigation.cs` already uses `shipStats.BaseSpeed` in the `MoveTowardsTarget()` method. However, the task mentions "speed clamping" which suggests we need to ensure the speed doesn't exceed a maximum value or is properly constrained.

Looking at the current implementation:
```csharp
float speed = shipStats != null ? shipStats.BaseSpeed : 1f;
```

There's no clamping here. The speed is simply taken from `ShipStats.BaseSpeed`. To implement "speed clamping", we need to:
1. Add a maximum speed field in `ShipStats` or `ShipNavigation`
2. Clamp the actual movement speed to not exceed this maximum

However, looking at the TODO.md context and the existing code structure, I believe the intent is to ensure the speed value is properly constrained. Since `ShipStats.BaseSpeed` is already a serialized field that can be set in the Inspector, the clamping might mean we should ensure the speed doesn't go below 0 or above some reasonable maximum.

Let me implement this by modifying `ShipNavigation.cs` to clamp the speed to a minimum of 0 and a maximum value. I'll add a `maxSpeed` field and clamp the speed between 0 and maxSpeed.

Here are the changes needed:

**Modify Assets\Scripts\Navigation\ShipNavigation.cs:**

1. Add a new serialized field for maximum speed:
```csharp
[SerializeField] private float maxSpeed = 10f;
```

2. Modify the `MoveTowardsTarget()` method to clamp the speed:
```csharp
private void MoveTowardsTarget()
{
    Vector2 currentPosition = transform.position;
    Vector2 targetPosition = targetPort.Coordinates;

    float distance = Vector2.Distance(currentPosition, targetPosition);
    
    if (distance <= arrivalThreshold)
    {
        isMoving = false;
        Debug.Log($"Arrived at {targetPort.PortName}");
        return;
    }

    float speed = shipStats != null ? shipStats.BaseSpeed : 1f;
    // Clamp the speed to ensure it's within valid bounds
    speed = Mathf.Clamp(speed, 0f, maxSpeed);
    
    Vector2 direction = (targetPosition - currentPosition).normalized;
    Vector2 movement = direction * speed * Time.deltaTime;
    
    transform.position += new Vector3(movement.x, movement.y, 0);
}
```

Alternatively, if the intent is to clamp the base speed in `ShipStats` itself, we could modify `ShipStats.cs` to clamp the `baseSpeed` value in its setter. But based on the TODO.md saying "Add speed clamping in ShipNavigation", I believe the first approach is correct.

Let me implement the changes to `ShipNavigation.cs`:

```csharp
using UnityEngine;

namespace PirateGame.Navigation
{
    public class ShipNavigation : MonoBehaviour
    {
        [SerializeField] private Port targetPort;
        [SerializeField] private float rotationSpeed = 5f;
        [SerializeField] private float arrivalThreshold = 0.5f;
        [SerializeField] private float maxSpeed = 10f; // Added max speed field

        private ShipStats shipStats;
        private bool isMoving = false;

        void Start()
        {
            shipStats = GetComponent<ShipStats>();
            if (shipStats == null)
            {
                Debug.LogError("ShipStats component not found on the same GameObject!");
            }
        }

        void Update()
        {
            if (targetPort == null || !isMoving) return;

            MoveTowardsTarget();
            RotateTowardsTarget();
        }

        public void SetTargetPort(Port port)
        {
            targetPort = port;
            isMoving = true;
        }

        private void MoveTowardsTarget()
        {
            Vector2 currentPosition = transform.position;
            Vector2 targetPosition = targetPort.Coordinates;

            float distance = Vector2.Distance(currentPosition, targetPosition);
            
            if (distance <= arrivalThreshold)
            {
                isMoving = false;
                Debug.Log($"Arrived at {targetPort.PortName}");
                return;
            }

            float speed = shipStats != null ? shipStats.BaseSpeed : 1f;
            // Clamp speed to ensure it's within valid bounds (0 to maxSpeed)
            speed = Mathf.Clamp(speed, 0f, maxSpeed);
            
            Vector2 direction = (targetPosition - currentPosition).normalized;
            Vector2 movement = direction * speed * Time.deltaTime;
            
            transform.position += new Vector3(movement.x, movement.y, 0);
        }

        private void RotateTowardsTarget()
        {
            Vector2 currentPosition = transform.position;
            Vector2 targetPosition = targetPort.Coordinates;
            
            Vector2 direction = targetPosition - currentPosition;
            float angle = Mathf.Atan2(direction.y, direction.x) * Mathf.Rad2Deg;
            
            Quaternion targetRotation = Quaternion.AngleAxis(angle, Vector3.forward);
            transform.rotation = Quaternion.Slerp(transform.rotation, targetRotation, rotationSpeed * Time.deltaTime);
        }

        public bool IsMoving()
        {
            return isMoving;
        }

        public Port GetCurrentTarget()
        {
            return targetPort;
        }
    }
}
```

```csharp
            {

            RotateTowardsTarget();
        }

        {

            isMoving = true;

            {

                return;

using UnityEngine;

namespace PirateGame.Navigation
{
    public class ShipNavigation : MonoBehaviour
    {
        [SerializeField] private Port targetPort;
        [SerializeField] private float rotationSpeed = 5f;
        [SerializeField] private float arrivalThreshold = 0.5f;
        [SerializeField] private float maxSpeed = 10f;

        private ShipStats shipStats;
        private bool isMoving = false;

        void Start()
        {
            shipStats = GetComponent<ShipStats>();
            if (shipStats == null)
            {
                Debug.LogError("ShipStats component not found on the same GameObject!");
            }
        }

        void Update()
        {
            if (targetPort == null || !isMoving) return;

            MoveTowardsTarget();
            RotateTowardsTarget();
        }

        public void SetTargetPort(Port port)
        {
            targetPort = port;
            isMoving = true;
        }

        private void MoveTowardsTarget()
        {
            Vector2 currentPosition = transform.position;
            Vector2 targetPosition = targetPort.Coordinates;

            float distance = Vector2.Distance(currentPosition, targetPosition);
            
            if (distance <= arrivalThreshold)
            {
                isMoving = false;
                Debug.Log($"Arrived at {targetPort.PortName}");
                return;
            }

            float speed = shipStats != null ? shipStats.BaseSpeed : 1f;
            speed = Mathf.Clamp(speed, 0f, maxSpeed);
            
            Vector2 direction = (targetPosition - currentPosition).normalized;
            Vector2 movement = direction * speed * Time.deltaTime;
            
            transform.position += new Vector3(movement.x, movement.y, 0);
        }

        private void RotateTowardsTarget()
        {
            Vector2 currentPosition = transform.position;
            Vector2 targetPosition = targetPort.Coordinates;
            
            Vector2 direction = targetPosition - currentPosition;
            float angle = Mathf.Atan2(direction.y, direction.x) * Mathf.Rad2Deg;

        }

        public bool IsMoving()
        {
            return isMoving;
        }

            return targetPort;
        }
    }
```

Looking at TODO.md, the first task marked with [ ] is:

**"Create PortEconomy.cs. It should store a list of prices for different ItemData."**

I'll implement this task. First, I need to understand the requirements:

1. Create `PortEconomy.cs` script
2. It should store a list of prices for different ItemData
3. Should be in the `PirateGame.Core` namespace (based on your rules)
4. Use `[SerializeField]` for serialized fields
5. Comments in English

Let me create the PortEconomy.cs file:

```csharp
using UnityEngine;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using PirateGame.Economy;

namespace PirateGame.Core
{
    public class PortEconomy : MonoBehaviour
    {
        // Dictionary to store item prices at this port
        // Key: ItemData reference, Value: Current price at this port
        [SerializeField] private List<ItemPrice> itemPrices = new List<ItemPrice>();

        // Method to get the price of a specific item at this port
        public int GetItemPrice(ItemData item)
        {
            foreach (var itemPrice in itemPrices)
            {
                if (itemPrice.item == item)
                {
                    return itemPrice.price;
                }
            }
            return 0; // Return 0 if item not found in this port's economy
        }

        // Method to set or update the price of an item at this port
        public void SetItemPrice(ItemData item, int price)
        {
            for (int i = 0; i < itemPrices.Count; i++)
            {
                if (itemPrices[i].item == item)
                {
                    itemPrices[i] = new ItemPrice { item = item, price = price };
                    return;
                }
            }
            // If item not found, add it to the list
            itemPrices.Add(new ItemPrice { item = item, price = price });
        }

        // Method to get all available items and their prices at this port
        public List<ItemPrice> GetAllItemPrices()
        {
            return new List<ItemPrice>(itemPrices);
        }

        // Helper method to initialize with default prices based on ItemData base values
        public void InitializeWithDefaultPrices(List<ItemData> availableItems)
        {
            foreach (var item in availableItems)
            {
                // Set initial price as base value with some random variation
                int price = Mathf.RoundToInt(item.BaseValue * Random.Range(0.8f, 1.2f));
                SetItemPrice(item, price);
            }
        }
    }

    // Serializable struct to store item-price pairs
    [System.Serializable]
    public struct ItemPrice
    {
        public ItemData item;
        public int price;
    }
}
```

Looking at the folder structure, economy-related scripts seem to be in Assets/Scripts/Economy/. However, the TODO.md mentions "PortEconomy.cs" without specifying a namespace. Since it's related to economy, I'll place it in the PirateGame.Economy namespace to match ItemData.cs.

Assets/Scripts/Economy/PortEconomy.cs
```csharp
<<<<<<< SEARCH
=======
using UnityEngine;
using System.Collections.Generic;

namespace PirateGame.Economy
{
    public class PortEconomy : MonoBehaviour
    {
        [System.Serializable]
        public struct ItemPrice
        {
            public ItemData item;
            public int price;
        }

        [SerializeField] private List<ItemPrice> itemPrices = new List<ItemPrice>();

        public int GetItemPrice(ItemData item)
        {
            foreach (ItemPrice itemPrice in itemPrices)
            {
                if (itemPrice.item == item)
                {
                    return itemPrice.price;
                }
            }
            return 0;
        }

        public void SetItemPrice(ItemData item, int price)
        {
            for (int i = 0; i < itemPrices.Count; i++)
            {
                if (itemPrices[i].item == item)
                {
                    ItemPrice updated = itemPrices[i];
                    updated.price = price;
                    itemPrices[i] = updated;
                    return;
                }
            }
            itemPrices.Add(new ItemPrice { item = item, price = price });
        }

        public List<ItemPrice> GetAllItemPrices()
        {
            return new List<ItemPrice>(itemPrices);
        }

        public void InitializeWithDefaultPrices(List<ItemData> availableItems)
        {
            foreach (ItemData item in availableItems)
            {
                int price = Mathf.RoundToInt(item.BaseValue * Random.Range(0.8f, 1.2f));
                SetItemPrice(item, price);
            }
        }
    }
}
```

**Step 1: Create Ship.cs in Assets\Scripts\Core\**

```csharp
using UnityEngine;
using PirateGame.Economy;

namespace PirateGame.Core
{
    public class Ship : MonoBehaviour
    {
        [SerializeField] private ShipStats shipStats;
        
        private void Start()
        {
            // Auto-get ShipStats if not assigned
            if (shipStats == null)
            {
                shipStats = GetComponent<ShipStats>();
            }
            
            if (shipStats == null)
            {
                Debug.LogError("ShipStats component not found on the same GameObject!");
            }
        }
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Attempt to buy an item from a port economy.
        /// Checks if ship has enough gold and cargo capacity.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="item">The item to buy</param>
        /// <param name="portEconomy">The port's economy system</param>
        /// <returns>True if purchase was successful, false otherwise</returns>
        public bool BuyItem(ItemData item, PortEconomy portEconomy)
        {
            if (shipStats == null || item == null || portEconomy == null)
            {
                Debug.LogWarning("Cannot buy item: Missing required components");
                return false;
            }
            
            int price = portEconomy.GetItemPrice(item);
            
            // Check if ship has enough gold
            if (shipStats.Gold < price)
            {
                Debug.Log($"Not enough gold to buy {item.ItemName}. Need {price}, have {shipStats.Gold}");
                return false;
            }
            
            // Check cargo capacity (assuming 1 unit per item)
            // Note: This is a simple implementation. You might want a cargo inventory system
            if (shipStats.CargoCapacity <= 0)
            {
                Debug.Log($"No cargo capacity available to buy {item.ItemName}");
                return false;
            }
            
            // Deduct gold
            shipStats.Gold -= price;
            
            // Reduce cargo capacity (simple implementation)
            shipStats.CargoCapacity -= 1;
            
            Debug.Log($"Bought {item.ItemName} for {price} gold. Remaining gold: {shipStats.Gold}, Cargo capacity: {shipStats.CargoCapacity}");
            return true;
        }
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Attempt to sell an item to a port economy.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="item">The item to sell</param>
        /// <param name="portEconomy">The port's economy system</param>
        /// <returns>True if sale was successful, false otherwise</returns>
        public bool SellItem(ItemData item, PortEconomy portEconomy)
        {
            if (shipStats == null || item == null || portEconomy == null)
            {
                Debug.LogWarning("Cannot sell item: Missing required components");
                return false;
            }
            
            int price = portEconomy.GetItemPrice(item);
            
            // Check if ship has cargo to sell (simple implementation)
            // In a real system, you'd check if the item is actually in the cargo hold
            if (shipStats.CargoCapacity >= 100) // Arbitrary max capacity check
            {
                Debug.Log($"No {item.ItemName} in cargo to sell");
                return false;
            }
            
            // Add gold
            shipStats.Gold += price;
            
            // Increase cargo capacity (freeing up space)
            shipStats.CargoCapacity += 1;
            
            Debug.Log($"Sold {item.ItemName} for {price} gold. Total gold: {shipStats.Gold}, Cargo capacity: {shipStats.CargoCapacity}");
            return true;
        }
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Get the ship's current gold amount
        /// </summary>
        public int GetGold()
        {
            return shipStats != null ? shipStats.Gold : 0;
        }
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Get the ship's current cargo capacity
        /// </summary>
        public int GetCargoCapacity()
        {
            return shipStats != null ? shipStats.CargoCapacity : 0;
        }
    }
}
```

namespace PirateGame.Core
{
    public class Ship : MonoBehaviour
    {
        [SerializeField] private ShipStats shipStats;
        
        private void Start()
        {
            // Auto-get ShipStats if not assigned
            if (shipStats == null)
            {
                shipStats = GetComponent<ShipStats>();
            }
            
            if (shipStats == null)
            {
                Debug.LogError("ShipStats component not found on the same GameObject!");
            }
        }
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Attempt to buy an item from a port economy.
        /// Checks if ship has enough gold and cargo capacity.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="item">The item to buy</param>
        /// <param name="portEconomy">The port's economy system</param>
        /// <returns>True if purchase was successful, false otherwise</returns>
        public bool BuyItem(ItemData item, PortEconomy portEconomy)
        {
            if (shipStats == null || item == null || portEconomy == null)
            {
                Debug.LogWarning("Cannot buy item: Missing required components");
                return false;
            }
            
            int price = portEconomy.GetItemPrice(item);
            
            // Check if ship has enough gold
            if (shipStats.Gold < price)
            {
                Debug.Log($"Not enough gold to buy {item.ItemName}. Need {price}, have {shipStats.Gold}");
                return false;
            }
            
            // Check cargo capacity (assuming 1 unit per item)
            // Note: This is a simple implementation. You might want a cargo inventory system
            if (shipStats.CargoCapacity <= 0)
            {
                Debug.Log($"No cargo capacity available to buy {item.ItemName}");
                return false;
            }
            
            // Deduct gold
            shipStats.Gold -= price;
            
            // Reduce cargo capacity (simple implementation)
            shipStats.CargoCapacity -= 1;
            
            Debug.Log($"Bought {item.ItemName} for {price} gold. Remaining gold: {shipStats.Gold}, Cargo capacity: {shipStats.CargoCapacity}");
            return true;
        }
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Attempt to sell an item to a port economy.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="item">The item to sell</param>
        /// <param name="portEconomy">The port's economy system</param>
        /// <returns>True if sale was successful, false otherwise</returns>
        public bool SellItem(ItemData item, PortEconomy portEconomy)
        {
            if (shipStats == null || item == null || portEconomy == null)
            {
                Debug.LogWarning("Cannot sell item: Missing required components");
                return false;
            }
            
            int price = portEconomy.GetItemPrice(item);
            
            // Check if ship has cargo to sell (simple implementation)
            // In a real system, you'd check if the item is actually in the cargo hold
            // For now, we'll assume the ship always has items to sell if there's capacity used
            // This is a placeholder implementation
            if (shipStats.CargoCapacity >= 100) // Assuming 100 is max capacity
            {
                Debug.Log($"No cargo capacity used to sell items");
                return false;
            }
            
            // Add gold
            shipStats.Gold += price;
            
            // Increase cargo capacity (freeing up space)
            shipStats.CargoCapacity += 1;
            
            Debug.Log($"Sold {item.ItemName} for {price} gold. Total gold: {shipStats.Gold}, Cargo capacity: {shipStats.CargoCapacity}");
            return true;

Looking at TODO.md, the first task marked with [ ] is:

```
[ ] Create HUDManager.cs to display Current Gold and Cargo status on the screen.
```

I need to implement this task. Based on the requirements:
1. Create `HUDManager.cs` in the `PirateGame.Core` namespace
2. Use `[SerializeField]` for fields
3. Display Current Gold and Cargo status on screen
4. Comments in English

Let me create the implementation:

```csharp
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.UI;

namespace PirateGame.Core
{
    public class HUDManager : MonoBehaviour
    {
        [SerializeField] private Ship ship;
        [SerializeField] private Text goldText;
        [SerializeField] private Text cargoText;
        
        private void Start()
        {
            // Try to find Ship component if not assigned
            if (ship == null)
            {
                ship = FindObjectOfType<Ship>();
            }
            
            if (ship == null)
            {
                Debug.LogError("HUDManager: No Ship component found in the scene!");
            }
            
            // Check if UI Text components are assigned
            if (goldText == null || cargoText == null)
            {
                Debug.LogError("HUDManager: GoldText or CargoText not assigned!");
            }
        }
        
        private void Update()
        {
            if (ship == null || goldText == null || cargoText == null) return;
            
            // Update gold display
            int currentGold = ship.GetGold();
            goldText.text = $"Gold: {currentGold}";
            
            // Update cargo display
            int currentCargo = ship.GetCargoCapacity();
            cargoText.text = $"Cargo: {currentCargo}";
        }
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Set the ship reference for the HUD manager
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="targetShip">The ship to track</param>
        public void SetShip(Ship targetShip)
        {
            ship = targetShip;
        }
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Set the UI Text component for displaying gold
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="textComponent">The Text component for gold display</param>
        public void SetGoldText(Text textComponent)
        {
            goldText = textComponent;
        }
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Set the UI Text component for displaying cargo status
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="textComponent">The Text component for cargo display</param>
        public void SetCargoText(Text textComponent)
        {
            cargoText = textComponent;
        }
    }
}
```

Now I need to run the build command to verify it compiles. Please run:

```
'C:\Program Files\Unity\Hub\Editor\2022.3.0f1\Editor\Unity.exe -batchmode -projectPath C:\Users\Admin\TradePirates -quit -logFile C:\Users\Admin\TradePirates\build.log'
```

After running this command, check the `build.log` file for any errors. If there are errors, I'll fix them. If the build is clean, I'll mark the task as [x] in TODO.md and commit with a clear message.

Actually, since we're in the PirateGame.UI namespace, and Ship is in PirateGame.Core, we need to either:

Assets/Scripts/UI/HUDManager.cs
```csharp
<<<<<<< SEARCH
=======
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.UI;
using PirateGame.Core;

namespace PirateGame.UI
{
    public class HUDManager : MonoBehaviour
    {
        [SerializeField] private Ship ship;
        [SerializeField] private Text goldText;
        [SerializeField] private Text cargoText;
        
        private void Start()
        {
            // Try to find Ship component if not assigned
            if (ship == null)
            {
                ship = FindObjectOfType<Ship>();
            }
            
            if (ship == null)
            {
                Debug.LogError("HUDManager: No Ship component found in the scene!");
            }
            
            // Check if UI Text components are assigned
```

2. Duplicate class definitions

The current HUDManager.cs needs to be fixed. Here are the changes needed:

**File: Assets\Scripts\UI\HUDManager.cs**

```csharp
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.UI;
using PirateGame.Core;

namespace PirateGame.UI
{
    public class HUDManager : MonoBehaviour
    {
        [SerializeField] private Ship ship;
        [SerializeField] private Text goldText;
        [SerializeField] private Text cargoText;
        
        private void Start()
        {
            // Try to find Ship component if not assigned
            if (ship == null)
            {
                ship = FindObjectOfType<Ship>();
            }
            
            if (ship == null)
            {
                Debug.LogError("HUDManager: No Ship component found in the scene!");
            }
            
            // Check if UI Text components are assigned
            if (goldText == null || cargoText == null)
            {
                Debug.LogError("HUDManager: GoldText or CargoText not assigned!");
            }
        }
        
        private void Update()
        {
            if (ship == null || goldText == null || cargoText == null) return;
            
            // Update gold display
            int currentGold = ship.GetGold();
            goldText.text = $"Gold: {currentGold}";
            
            // Update cargo display
            int currentCargo = ship.GetCargoCapacity();
            cargoText.text = $"Cargo: {currentCargo}";
        }
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Set the ship reference for the HUD manager
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="targetShip">The ship to track</param>
        public void SetShip(Ship targetShip)
        {
            ship = targetShip;
        }
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Set the UI Text component for displaying gold
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="textComponent">The Text component for gold display</param>
        public void SetGoldText(Text textComponent)
        {
            goldText = textComponent;
        }
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Set the UI Text component for displaying cargo status
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="textComponent">The Text component for cargo display</param>
        public void SetCargoText(Text textComponent)
        {
            cargoText = textComponent;
        }
    }
}
```

**Changes made:**
1. Removed the duplicate namespace declaration at the top
2. Removed the duplicate class definition that was appended at the end
3. Ensured proper using statements: `using PirateGame.Core;` for the Ship class
4. Kept all the functionality intact

This HUDManager.cs file now:
- Uses the correct namespace `PirateGame.UI`
- Has proper `using` statements
- Displays current gold and cargo status on the screen
- Follows all the rules: uses `[SerializeField]`, comments in English

{
    public class HUDManager : MonoBehaviour
    {
        [SerializeField] private Core.Ship ship;
        [SerializeField] private Text goldText;
        [SerializeField] private Text cargoText;
        
        private void Start()
        {
            // Try to find Ship component if not assigned
            if (ship == null)
            {
                ship = FindObjectOfType<Core.Ship>();
            }
            
            if (ship == null)
            {
                Debug.LogError("HUDManager: No Ship component found in the scene!");
            }

            {
                Debug.LogError("HUDManager: GoldText or CargoText not assigned!");
            }

Since the READ ONLY version already shows a complete implementation, I'll create the same file. Here's the code for `HUDManager.cs`:

```csharp
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.UI;
using PirateGame.Core;

namespace PirateGame.UI
{
    public class HUDManager : MonoBehaviour
    {
        [SerializeField] private Ship ship;
        [SerializeField] private Text goldText;
        [SerializeField] private Text cargoText;
        
        private void Start()
        {
            // Try to find Ship component if not assigned
            if (ship == null)
            {
                ship = FindObjectOfType<Ship>();
            }
            
            if (ship == null)
            {
                Debug.LogError("HUDManager: No Ship component found in the scene!");
            }
            
            // Check if UI Text components are assigned
            if (goldText == null || cargoText == null)
            {
                Debug.LogError("HUDManager: GoldText or CargoText not assigned!");
            }
        }
        
        private void Update()
        {
            if (ship == null || goldText == null || cargoText == null) return;
            
            // Update gold display
            int currentGold = ship.GetGold();
            goldText.text = $"Gold: {currentGold}";
            
            // Update cargo display
            int currentCargo = ship.GetCargoCapacity();
            cargoText.text = $"Cargo: {currentCargo}";
        }
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Set the ship reference for the HUD manager
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="targetShip">The ship to track</param>
        public void SetShip(Ship targetShip)
        {
            ship = targetShip;
        }
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Set the UI Text component for displaying gold
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="textComponent">The Text component for gold display</param>
        public void SetGoldText(Text textComponent)
        {
            goldText = textComponent;
        }
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Set the UI Text component for displaying cargo status
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="textComponent">The Text component for cargo display</param>
        public void SetCargoText(Text textComponent)
        {
            cargoText = textComponent;
        }
    }
}
```

This task is in the "Basic UI" section. I need to implement a UI notification system that triggers when the ship arrives at a port.

Based on the current code structure, I need to:
1. Create a UI notification system that can display messages
2. Connect it to the ship's arrival event in ShipNavigation.cs
3. Follow the namespace and serialization requirements

Let me implement this step by step:

**Step 1: Create a UI notification script**

I'll create a new script `UINotification.cs` in the `PirateGame.UI` namespace:

```csharp
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.UI;

namespace PirateGame.UI
{
    public class UINotification : MonoBehaviour
    {
        [SerializeField] private Text notificationText;
        [SerializeField] private float displayDuration = 3f;
        [SerializeField] private float fadeDuration = 0.5f;

        private CanvasGroup canvasGroup;
        private float timer = 0f;
        private bool isShowing = false;

        private void Start()
        {
            canvasGroup = GetComponent<CanvasGroup>();
            if (canvasGroup == null)
            {
                canvasGroup = gameObject.AddComponent<CanvasGroup>();
            }

            // Start hidden
            canvasGroup.alpha = 0f;
            gameObject.SetActive(false);
        }

        private void Update()
        {
            if (!isShowing) return;

            timer += Time.deltaTime;

            if (timer <= fadeDuration)
            {
                // Fade in
                canvasGroup.alpha = Mathf.Lerp(0f, 1f, timer / fadeDuration);
            }
            else if (timer >= displayDuration - fadeDuration)
            {
                // Fade out
                float fadeOutTime = timer - (displayDuration - fadeDuration);
                canvasGroup.alpha = Mathf.Lerp(1f, 0f, fadeOutTime / fadeDuration);
            }

            if (timer >= displayDuration)
            {
                HideNotification();
            }
        }

        public void ShowNotification(string message)
        {
            if (notificationText != null)
            {
                notificationText.text = message;
            }

            gameObject.SetActive(true);
            isShowing = true;
            timer = 0f;
            canvasGroup.alpha = 0f;
        }

        private void HideNotification()
        {
            isShowing = false;
            gameObject.SetActive(false);
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Set the Text component for displaying notifications
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="textComponent">The Text component for notifications</param>
        public void SetNotificationText(Text textComponent)
        {
            notificationText = textComponent;
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Set how long the notification should be displayed (in seconds)
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="duration">Display duration in seconds</param>
        public void SetDisplayDuration(float duration)
        {
            displayDuration = duration;
        }
```

```csharp
// Add this using statement at the top
using PirateGame.UI;

// Add this field to the ShipNavigation class
[SerializeField] private UINotification uiNotification;

// Modify the MoveTowardsTarget method to trigger notification
private void MoveTowardsTarget()
{
    Vector2 currentPosition = transform.position;
    Vector2 targetPosition = targetPort.Coordinates;

    float distance = Vector2.Distance(currentPosition, targetPosition);
    
    if (distance <= arrivalThreshold)
    {
        isMoving = false;
        Debug.Log($"Arrived at {targetPort.PortName}");
        
        // Trigger UI notification
        if (uiNotification != null)
        {
            uiNotification.ShowNotification($"Arrived at {targetPort.PortName}");
        }
        return;
    }

    float speed = shipStats != null ? shipStats.BaseSpeed : 1f;
    speed = Mathf.Clamp(speed, 0f, maxSpeed);
    
    Vector2 direction = (targetPosition - currentPosition).normalized;
    Vector2 movement = direction * speed * Time.deltaTime;
    
    transform.position += new Vector3(movement.x, movement.y, 0);
}

// Add this method to set the UI notification reference
public void SetUINotification(UINotification notification)
{
    uiNotification = notification;
}
```

1. First, create the new UINotification.cs file:

Assets/Scripts/UI/UINotification.cs
```csharp
<<<<<<< SEARCH
=======
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.UI;

namespace PirateGame.UI
{
    public class UINotification : MonoBehaviour
    {
        [SerializeField] private Text notificationText;
        [SerializeField] private float displayDuration = 3f;
        [SerializeField] private float fadeDuration = 0.5f;

        private CanvasGroup canvasGroup;
        private float timer = 0f;
        private bool isShowing = false;

        private void Start()
        {
            canvasGroup = GetComponent<CanvasGroup>();
            if (canvasGroup == null)
            {
                canvasGroup = gameObject.AddComponent<CanvasGroup>();
            }

            // Start hidden
            canvasGroup.alpha = 0f;
            gameObject.SetActive(false);
        }

        private void Update()
        {
            if (!isShowing) return;

            timer += Time.deltaTime;

            if (timer <= fadeDuration)
            {
                // Fade in
                canvasGroup.alpha = Mathf.Lerp(0f, 1f, timer / fadeDuration);
            }
            else if (timer >= displayDuration - fadeDuration)
            {
                // Fade out
                float fadeOutTime = timer - (displayDuration - fadeDuration);
                canvasGroup.alpha = Mathf.Lerp(1f, 0f, fadeOutTime / fadeDuration);
            }

            if (timer >= displayDuration)
            {
                HideNotification();
            }
        }

        public void ShowNotification(string message)
        {
            if (notificationText != null)
            {
                notificationText.text = message;
            }

            gameObject.SetActive(true);
            isShowing = true;
            timer = 0f;
            canvasGroup.alpha = 0f;
        }

        private void HideNotification()
        {
            isShowing = false;
            gameObject.SetActive(false);
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Set the Text component for displaying notifications
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="textComponent">The Text component for notifications</param>
        public void SetNotificationText(Text textComponent)
        {
            notificationText = textComponent;
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Set how long the notification should be displayed (in seconds)
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="duration">Display duration in seconds</param>
        public void SetDisplayDuration(float duration)
        {
            displayDuration = duration;
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Set how long the fade in/out should take (in seconds)
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="duration">Fade duration in seconds</param>
        public void SetFadeDuration(float duration)
        {
            fadeDuration = duration;
        }
    }
}
```

2. Next, modify ShipNavigation.cs to add the notification functionality:

Assets/Scripts/Navigation/ShipNavigation.cs
```csharp
<<<<<<< SEARCH
using UnityEngine;

namespace PirateGame.Navigation
{
    public class ShipNavigation : MonoBehaviour
    {
        [SerializeField] private Port targetPort;
        [SerializeField] private float rotationSpeed = 5f;
        [SerializeField] private float arrivalThreshold = 0.5f;
        [SerializeField] private float maxSpeed = 10f;

        private ShipStats shipStats;
        private bool isMoving = false;

        void Start()
        {
            shipStats = GetComponent<ShipStats>();
            if (shipStats == null)
            {
                Debug.LogError("ShipStats component not found on the same GameObject!");
            }
        }

        void Update()
        {
            if (targetPort == null || !isMoving) return;

            MoveTowardsTarget();
            RotateTowardsTarget();
        }

        public void SetTargetPort(Port port)
        {
            targetPort = port;
            isMoving = true;
        }

        private void MoveTowardsTarget()
        {
            Vector2 currentPosition = transform.position;
            Vector2 targetPosition = targetPort.Coordinates;

            float distance = Vector2.Distance(currentPosition, targetPosition);
            
            if (distance <= arrivalThreshold)
            {
                isMoving = false;
                Debug.Log($"Arrived at {targetPort.PortName}");
                return;
            }

            float speed = shipStats != null ? shipStats.BaseSpeed : 1f;
            speed = Mathf.Clamp(speed, 0f, maxSpeed);
            
            Vector2 direction = (targetPosition - currentPosition).normalized;
            Vector2 movement = direction * speed * Time.deltaTime;
            
            transform.position += new Vector3(movement.x, movement.y, 0);
        }

        private void RotateTowardsTarget()
        {
            Vector2 currentPosition = transform.position;
            Vector2 targetPosition = targetPort.Coordinates;
            
            Vector2 direction = targetPosition - currentPosition;
            float angle = Mathf.Atan2(direction.y, direction.x) * Mathf.Rad2Deg;
            
            Quaternion targetRotation = Quaternion.AngleAxis(angle, Vector3.forward);
            transform.rotation = Quaternion.Slerp(transform.rotation, targetRotation, rotationSpeed * Time.deltaTime);
        }

        public bool IsMoving()
        {
            return isMoving;
        }

        public Port GetCurrentTarget()
        {
            return targetPort;
        }
    }
}
=======
using UnityEngine;
using PirateGame.UI;

namespace PirateGame.Navigation
{
    public class ShipNavigation : MonoBehaviour
    {
        [SerializeField] private Port targetPort;
        [SerializeField] private float rotationSpeed = 5f;
        [SerializeField] private float arrivalThreshold = 0.5f;
        [SerializeField] private float maxSpeed = 10f;
        [SerializeField] private UINotification uiNotification;

        private ShipStats shipStats;
        private bool isMoving = false;

        void Start()
        {
            shipStats = GetComponent<ShipStats>();
            if (shipStats == null)
            {
                Debug.LogError("ShipStats component not found on the same GameObject!");
            }
        }

        void Update()
        {
            if (targetPort == null || !isMoving) return;

            MoveTowardsTarget();
            RotateTowardsTarget();
        }

        public void SetTargetPort(Port port)
        {
            targetPort = port;
            isMoving = true;
        }

        private void MoveTowardsTarget()
        {
            Vector2 currentPosition = transform.position;
            Vector2 targetPosition = targetPort.Coordinates;

            float distance = Vector2.Distance(currentPosition, targetPosition);
            
            if (distance <= arrivalThreshold)
            {
                isMoving = false;
                Debug.Log($"Arrived at {targetPort.PortName}");
                
                // Trigger UI notification
                if (uiNotification != null)
                {
                    uiNotification.ShowNotification($"Arrived at {targetPort.PortName}");
                }
                return;
            }

            float speed = shipStats != null ? shipStats.BaseSpeed : 1f;
            speed = Mathf.Clamp(speed, 0f, maxSpeed);
            
            Vector2 direction = (targetPosition - currentPosition).normalized;
            Vector2 movement = direction * speed * Time.deltaTime;
            
            transform.position += new Vector3(movement.x, movement.y, 0);
        }

        private void RotateTowardsTarget()
        {
            Vector2 currentPosition = transform.position;
            Vector2 targetPosition = targetPort.Coordinates;
            
            Vector2 direction = targetPosition - currentPosition;
            float angle = Mathf.Atan2(direction.y, direction.x) * Mathf.Rad2Deg;
            
            Quaternion targetRotation = Quaternion.AngleAxis(angle, Vector3.forward);
            transform.rotation = Quaternion.Slerp(transform.rotation, targetRotation, rotationSpeed * Time.deltaTime);
        }

        public bool IsMoving()
        {
            return isMoving;
        }

        public Port GetCurrentTarget()
        {
            return targetPort;
        }

        public void SetUINotification(UINotification notification)
        {
            uiNotification = notification;
        }
    }
}
```

```csharp
        [System.Serializable]
        public struct ItemPrice
        {
            public ItemData item;
            public int price;
        }

        [SerializeField] private List<ItemPrice> itemPrices = new List<ItemPrice>();

        public int GetItemPrice(ItemData item)
        {
            foreach (ItemPrice itemPrice in itemPrices)
            {
                if (itemPrice.item == item)
                {
                    return itemPrice.price;
                }
            }
            return 0;
        }

        public void SetItemPrice(ItemData item, int price)
        {
            for (int i = 0; i < itemPrices.Count; i++)
            {
                if (itemPrices[i].item == item)
                {
                    ItemPrice updated = itemPrices[i];
                    updated.price = price;
                    itemPrices[i] = updated;
                    return;
                }
            }
            itemPrices.Add(new ItemPrice { item = item, price = price });
        }

        public List<ItemPrice> GetAllItemPrices()
        {
            return new List<ItemPrice>(itemPrices);
        }

        public void InitializeWithDefaultPrices(List<ItemData> availableItems)
        {
            foreach (ItemData item in availableItems)
            {
                int price = Mathf.RoundToInt(item.BaseValue * Random.Range(0.8f, 1.2f));
                SetItemPrice(item, price);
            }
        }
    }
}
=======

using System.Collections.Generic;
using PirateGame.Core;

namespace PirateGame.Economy
{
    public class PortEconomy : MonoBehaviour
    {
        [System.Serializable]
        public struct ItemPrice
        {
            public ItemData item;
            public int price;
        }

        [SerializeField] private List<ItemPrice> itemPrices = new List<ItemPrice>();

        public int GetItemPrice(ItemData item)
        {
            foreach (ItemPrice itemPrice in itemPrices)
            {
                if (itemPrice.item == item)
                {
                    return itemPrice.price;
                }
            }
            return 0;
        }

        public void SetItemPrice(ItemData item, int price)
        {
            for (int i = 0; i < itemPrices.Count; i++)
            {
                if (itemPrices[i].item == item)
                {
                    ItemPrice updated = itemPrices[i];
                    updated.price = price;
                    itemPrices[i] = updated;
                    return;
                }
            }
            itemPrices.Add(new ItemPrice { item = item, price = price });
        }

        public List<ItemPrice> GetAllItemPrices()
        {
            return new List<ItemPrice>(itemPrices);
        }

        public void InitializeWithDefaultPrices(List<ItemData> availableItems)
        {
            foreach (ItemData item in availableItems)
            {
                int price = Mathf.RoundToInt(item.BaseValue * Random.Range(0.8f, 1.2f));
                SetItemPrice(item, price);
            }
        }
    }
```

This duplication can cause compilation errors because the same class name exists in two different namespaces, and other scripts might reference the wrong one.

Since the TODO.md specifies that ItemData.cs should be created as a ScriptableObject, and it's marked as complete, having two versions is likely an oversight. The TODO.md doesn't specify which namespace to use, but looking at the structure:
- ShipStats.cs is in PirateGame.Core
- Port.cs is in PirateGame.Navigation  
- PortEconomy.cs is in PirateGame.Economy
- Ship.cs is in PirateGame.Core

2. Ship.cs uses ItemData without any using statement, so it expects ItemData to be in PirateGame.Core

```csharp
using UnityEngine;
using PirateGame.Economy;

namespace PirateGame.Core
{
    public class Ship : MonoBehaviour
    {
        [SerializeField] private ShipStats shipStats;
        
        private void Start()
        {
            // Auto-get ShipStats if not assigned
            if (shipStats == null)
            {
                shipStats = GetComponent<ShipStats>();
            }
            
            if (shipStats == null)
            {
                Debug.LogError("ShipStats component not found on the same GameObject!");
            }
        }
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Attempt to buy an item from a port economy.
        /// Checks if ship has enough gold and cargo capacity.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="item">The item to buy</param>
        /// <param name="portEconomy">The port's economy system</param>
        /// <returns>True if purchase was successful, false otherwise</returns>
        public bool BuyItem(ItemData item, PortEconomy portEconomy)
        {
            if (shipStats == null || item == null || portEconomy == null)
            {
                Debug.LogWarning("Cannot buy item: Missing required components");
                return false;
            }
            
            int price = portEconomy.GetItemPrice(item);
            
            // Check if ship has enough gold
            if (shipStats.Gold < price)
            {
                Debug.Log($"Not enough gold to buy {item.ItemName}. Need {price}, have {shipStats.Gold}");
                return false;
            }
            
            // Check cargo capacity (assuming 1 unit per item)
            // Note: This is a simple implementation. You might want a cargo inventory system
            if (shipStats.CargoCapacity <= 0)
            {
                Debug.Log($"No cargo capacity available to buy {item.ItemName}");
                return false;
            }
            
            // Deduct gold
            shipStats.Gold -= price;
            
            // Reduce cargo capacity (simple implementation)
            shipStats.CargoCapacity -= 1;
            
            Debug.Log($"Bought {item.ItemName} for {price} gold. Remaining gold: {shipStats.Gold}, Cargo capacity: {shipStats.CargoCapacity}");
            return true;
        }
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Attempt to sell an item to a port economy.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="item">The item to sell</param>
        /// <param name="portEconomy">The port's economy system</param>
        /// <returns>True if sale was successful, false otherwise</returns>
        public bool SellItem(ItemData item, PortEconomy portEconomy)
        {
            if (shipStats == null || item == null || portEconomy == null)
            {
                Debug.LogWarning("Cannot sell item: Missing required components");
                return false;
            }
            
            int price = portEconomy.GetItemPrice(item);
            
            // Check if ship has cargo to sell (simple implementation)
            // In a real system, you'd check if the item is actually in the cargo hold
            // For now, we'll assume the ship always has items to sell if there's capacity used
            // This is a placeholder implementation
            if (shipStats.CargoCapacity >= 100) // Assuming 100 is max capacity
            {
                Debug.Log($"No cargo capacity used to sell items");
                return false;
            }
            
            // Add gold
            shipStats.Gold += price;
            
            // Increase cargo capacity (freeing up space)
            shipStats.CargoCapacity += 1;
            
            Debug.Log($"Sold {item.ItemName} for {price} gold. Total gold: {shipStats.Gold}, Cargo capacity: {shipStats.CargoCapacity}");
            return true;
        }
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Get the ship's current gold amount
        /// </summary>
        public int GetGold()
        {
            return shipStats != null ? shipStats.Gold : 0;
        }
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Get the ship's current cargo capacity
        /// </summary>
        public int GetCargoCapacity()
        {
            return shipStats != null ? shipStats.CargoCapacity : 0;
        }
    }
}

using UnityEngine;
using PirateGame.Economy;

namespace PirateGame.Core
{
    public class Ship : MonoBehaviour
    {
        [SerializeField] private ShipStats shipStats;
        
        private void Start()
        {
            // Auto-get ShipStats if not assigned
            if (shipStats == null)
            {
                shipStats = GetComponent<ShipStats>();
            }
            
            if (shipStats == null)
            {
                Debug.LogError("ShipStats component not found on the same GameObject!");
            }
        }
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Attempt to buy an item from a port economy.
        /// Checks if ship has enough gold and cargo capacity.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="item">The item to buy</param>
        /// <param name="portEconomy">The port's economy system</param>
        /// <returns>True if purchase was successful, false otherwise</returns>
        public bool BuyItem(PirateGame.Economy.ItemData item, PortEconomy portEconomy)
        {
            if (shipStats == null || item == null || portEconomy == null)
            {
                Debug.LogWarning("Cannot buy item: Missing required components");
                return false;
            }
            
            int price = portEconomy.GetItemPrice(item);
            
            // Check if ship has enough gold
            if (shipStats.Gold < price)
            {
                Debug.Log($"Not enough gold to buy {item.ItemName}. Need {price}, have {shipStats.Gold}");
                return false;
            }
            
            // Check cargo capacity (assuming 1 unit per item)
            // Note: This is a simple implementation. You might want a cargo inventory system
            if (shipStats.CargoCapacity <= 0)
            {
                Debug.Log($"No cargo capacity available to buy {item.ItemName}");
                return false;
            }
            
            // Deduct gold
            shipStats.Gold -= price;
            
            // Reduce cargo capacity (simple implementation)
            shipStats.CargoCapacity -= 1;
            
            Debug.Log($"Bought {item.ItemName} for {price} gold. Remaining gold: {shipStats.Gold}, Cargo capacity: {shipStats.CargoCapacity}");
            return true;
        }
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Attempt to sell an item to a port economy.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="item">The item to sell</param>
        /// <param name="portEconomy">The port's economy system</param>
        /// <returns>True if sale was successful, false otherwise</returns>
        public bool SellItem(PirateGame.Economy.ItemData item, PortEconomy portEconomy)
        {
            if (shipStats == null || item == null || portEconomy == null)
            {
                Debug.LogWarning("Cannot sell item: Missing required components");
                return false;
            }
            
            int price = portEconomy.GetItemPrice(item);
            
            // Check if ship has cargo to sell (simple implementation)
            // In a real system, you'd check if the item is actually in the cargo hold
            // For now, we'll assume the ship always has items to sell if there's capacity used
            // This is a placeholder implementation
            if (shipStats.CargoCapacity >= 100) // Assuming 100 is max capacity
            {
                Debug.Log($"No cargo capacity used to sell items");
                return false;
            }
            
            // Add gold
            shipStats.Gold += price;
            
            // Increase cargo capacity (freeing up space)
            shipStats.CargoCapacity += 1;
            
            Debug.Log($"Sold {item.ItemName} for {price} gold. Total gold: {shipStats.Gold}, Cargo capacity: {shipStats.CargoCapacity}");
            return true;
        }
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Get the ship's current gold amount
        /// </summary>
        public int GetGold()
        {
            return shipStats != null ? shipStats.Gold : 0;
        }
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Get the ship's current cargo capacity
        /// </summary>
        public int GetCargoCapacity()
        {
            return shipStats != null ? shipStats.CargoCapacity : 0;
        }
    }
```

Looking at the code, I notice a few issues:

1. **Namespace Conflict**: There are two `ItemData` classes in different namespaces:
   - `PirateGame.Economy.ItemData`
   - `PirateGame.Core.ItemData`
   This can cause confusion and compilation errors.

2. **Ship Navigation Issues**: In `ShipNavigation.cs`, the `ShipStats` component is used, but `ShipStats` doesn't have a `BaseSpeed` property (it has a field with a property). Actually, looking at `ShipStats.cs`, it does have a `BaseSpeed` property, so this should be fine.

3. **HUDManager References**: `HUDManager.cs` references a `Ship` class, but it's trying to call `GetGold()` and `GetCargoCapacity()` which exist in the `Ship` class. However, `HUDManager.cs` doesn't have a `using PirateGame.Core;` statement, which might cause issues.

4. **SellItem Implementation**: The `SellItem` method in `Ship.cs` has a placeholder implementation that checks if `CargoCapacity >= 100`, which doesn't make sense. It should check if there's actually cargo to sell.

Since the TODO.md shows all tasks are complete, but there are implementation issues, I should fix these problems. Which issues would you like me to address first?

```csharp
using System;

namespace PirateGame.Core
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Represents the current high-level state of the game.
    /// </summary>
    public enum GameState
    {

        /// Player is at a port, can trade
        /// </summary>
        Port,
```

```csharp
<<<<<<< SEARCH
=======
using UnityEngine;
using System;

namespace PirateGame.Core
{
    public class GameStateManager : MonoBehaviour
    {
        [SerializeField] private GameState currentState = GameState.WorldMap;
        
        public GameState CurrentState => currentState;
        
        public event Action<GameState> OnStateEntered;
        public event Action<GameState> OnStateExited;
        
        public void ChangeState(GameState newState)
        {
            if (currentState == newState)
            {
                return;
            }
            
            OnStateExited?.Invoke(currentState);
            
            GameState previousState = currentState;
```

```csharp
            shipStats = GetComponent<ShipStats>();
            if (shipStats == null)
            {
                Debug.LogError("ShipStats component not found on the same GameObject!");

            if (gameStateManager == null)
            {
                gameStateManager = FindObjectOfType<GameStateManager>();
            }

            if (targetPort == null || !isMoving) return;

                isMoving = false;
```

```csharp
        private void MoveTowardsTarget()
        {
            Vector2 currentPosition = transform.position;
            Vector2 targetPosition = targetPort.Coordinates;

            float distance = Vector2.Distance(currentPosition, targetPosition);
            
            if (distance <= arrivalThreshold)
            {
                isMoving = false;
                Debug.Log($"Arrived at {targetPort.PortName}");
                
                // Change game state to Port
                if (gameStateManager != null)
                {
                    gameStateManager.ChangeState(GameState.Port);
                }
                
                // Trigger UI notification (kept for backward compatibility, but could be moved to UI manager)
                if (uiNotification != null)
                {
                    uiNotification.ShowNotification($"Arrived at {targetPort.PortName}");
                }
                return;
            }

            float speed = shipStats != null ? shipStats.BaseSpeed : 1f;
            speed = Mathf.Clamp(speed, 0f, maxSpeed);
            
            Vector2 direction = (targetPosition - currentPosition).normalized;
            Vector2 movement = direction * speed * Time.deltaTime;
            
            transform.position += new Vector3(movement.x, movement.y, 0);
```

Assets\Scripts\Core\GameStateManager.cs
```csharp
using UnityEngine;
using System;

namespace PirateGame.Core
{
    public class GameStateManager : MonoBehaviour
    {
        [SerializeField] private GameState currentState = GameState.WorldMap;
        
        public GameState CurrentState => currentState;
        
        public event Action<GameState> OnStateEntered;
        public event Action<GameState> OnStateExited;
        
        public void ChangeState(GameState newState)
        {
            if (currentState == newState)
            {
                return;
            }
            
            OnStateExited?.Invoke(currentState);
            
            GameState previousState = currentState;
            currentState = newState;
            
            #if UNITY_EDITOR
            Debug.Log($"GameState changed from {previousState} to {currentState}");
            #endif
            
            OnStateEntered?.Invoke(currentState);
        }
    }
}
```

This also matches all the requirements. So both tasks 5.1 and 5.2 are already implemented. However, TODO.md shows them as incomplete. Since the user hasn't provided TODO.md as an editable file, I can't update it.

Looking at the remaining tasks, I need to integrate with ShipNavigation, which is task 5.4. Let me check the current ShipNavigation.cs:

Assets\Scripts\Navigation\ShipNavigation.cs
```csharp
using UnityEngine;
using PirateGame.UI;
using PirateGame.Core;

namespace PirateGame.Navigation
{
    public class ShipNavigation : MonoBehaviour
    {
        [SerializeField] private Port targetPort;
        [SerializeField] private float rotationSpeed = 5f;
        [SerializeField] private float arrivalThreshold = 0.5f;
        [SerializeField] private float maxSpeed = 10f;
        [SerializeField] private UINotification uiNotification;
        [SerializeField] private GameStateManager gameStateManager;

        private ShipStats shipStats;
        private bool isMoving = false;

        void Start()
        {
            shipStats = GetComponent<ShipStats>();
            if (shipStats == null)
            {
                Debug.LogError("ShipStats component not found on the same GameObject!");
            }
            
            // Auto-find GameStateManager if not assigned
            if (gameStateManager == null)
            {
                gameStateManager = FindObjectOfType<GameStateManager>();
            }
        }

        void Update()
        {
            if (targetPort == null || !isMoving) return;
            
            // Block movement if not in WorldMap state
            if (gameStateManager != null && gameStateManager.CurrentState != GameState.WorldMap)
            {
                isMoving = false;
                return;
            }

            MoveTowardsTarget();
            RotateTowardsTarget();
        }

        public void SetTargetPort(Port port)
        {
            targetPort = port;
            isMoving = true;
        }

        private void MoveTowardsTarget()
        {
            Vector2 currentPosition = transform.position;
            Vector2 targetPosition = targetPort.Coordinates;

            float distance = Vector2.Distance(currentPosition, targetPosition);
            
            if (distance <= arrivalThreshold)
            {
                isMoving = false;
                Debug.Log($"Arrived at {targetPort.PortName}");
                
                // Change game state to Port
                if (gameStateManager != null)
                {
                    gameStateManager.ChangeState(GameState.Port);
                }
                
                // Trigger UI notification (kept for backward compatibility, but could be moved to UI manager)
                if (uiNotification != null)
                {
                    uiNotification.ShowNotification($"Arrived at {targetPort.PortName}");
                }
                return;
            }

            float speed = shipStats != null ? shipStats.BaseSpeed : 1f;
            speed = Mathf.Clamp(speed, 0f, maxSpeed);
            
            Vector2 direction = (targetPosition - currentPosition).normalized;
            Vector2 movement = direction * speed * Time.deltaTime;
            
            transform.position += new Vector3(movement.x, movement.y, 0);
        }

        private void RotateTowardsTarget()
        {
            Vector2 currentPosition = transform.position;
            Vector2 targetPosition = targetPort.Coordinates;
            
            Vector2 direction = targetPosition - currentPosition;
            float angle = Mathf.Atan2(direction.y, direction.x) * Mathf.Rad2Deg;
            
            Quaternion targetRotation = Quaternion.AngleAxis(angle, Vector3.forward);
            transform.rotation = Quaternion.Slerp(transform.rotation, targetRotation, rotationSpeed * Time.deltaTime);
        }

        public bool IsMoving()
        {
            return isMoving;
        }

        public Port GetCurrentTarget()
        {
            return targetPort;
        }

        public void SetUINotification(UINotification notification)
        {
            uiNotification = notification;
        }
    }
}
```

This already has the GameStateManager integration. However, TODO.md task 5.4 mentions using FixedUpdate() and setting Rigidbody2D velocity to zero. The current implementation uses Update() and doesn't have a Rigidbody2D. So this needs to be updated.

Also, task 5.5 mentions removing direct UI calls from ShipNavigation, but the current code still calls uiNotification.ShowNotification().
